NOTE: This is my experience using their website and not the actual location.

First time using 1-800-Flowers.  I was thinking to myself, wow its gotta be a hectic supply chain to get people exactly what they order since there are so many different varieties of flowers!

I ordered Weds night for a Friday delivery.  The order was not delivered on time.  I recommend not using them if you need flowers on a specific day/time.  Good chance they will fall short.

UPDATE:  I emailed them as I thought that would be the most effective way to get ahold of them.  Sure enough, I received a response that night (11pm). <date>1595627189717<//date>< Rating>

<Text>07-24-20: We've now had the Trailmaster Mid XRX assembled for a week.  Assembly was pretty self evident for an experienced mechanic or karter, but that is good because printed instructions for actual assembly are practically non-existent.  You can find videos for assembly on YouTube, though.  The first issue, which I consider to be a safety issue, was that the seat belt/harness system would not operate correctly.  One of my grandsons was stuck in the kart for 15 minutes before actually trying to drive it, while I tried to lubricate, and eventually pry the catch mechanism apart inside the belt.  In addition, it is extremely difficult to tighten the belts, thereby resulting in 12 year old boys not bothering to get them tightened correctly.  Finally, after the first 10-15 minutes of running, the engine began to sputter, then died and could not be restarted immediately.  It was as if it had run out of fuel.  So, my grandsons patiently waited about 15 minutes while I checked over the fuel system.  The supplied fuel filter is opaque, so it was very difficult to see if there was any fuel flowing.  After checking things over, we tried to start it again and it fired right up.  The boys rode it for another 10-15 minutes at which time it again began to sputter and died, just as it did the first time.  This time I examined the fuel filter more closely and determined that it had indeed starved itself of fuel.  I contacted Tech Support and two days later received a reply that the carburetor was probably dirty and the jets clogged.  In my over 40 years of being a mechanical engineer, kart racing and 20 years of restoring classic motorcycles, I have never had a dirty carburetor be the reason for an engine running fine for 10 minutes, then sputter and die, only to be fine again 15 minutes later.  Nevertheless, I tore down the carb, but while having it apart inspected the fuel line and petcock on the gas tank.  From my experience, they appeared to be very small, allowing only a trickle of gasoline.  But, I reassembled everything and once again it ran fine for 10 minutes then sputtered and died until we let it rest for 15 minutes whereupon it ran fine again for 10 minutes.  After contacting Tech Support again, two days later I received a reply that stated, "must be a bad jet".  This time I bought a new petcock and a clear fuel filter correctly sized for a 6.5 HP engine, and replaced all the undersized fuel line with 1/4" fuel line.  It's been running fine since and wearing out my grandsons.  No more short, 10 minutes on, 15 minutes off.  I had been planning on buying two more of these for my other grandson's families, but will reconsider another company.< /Text>< Resp>

<Review>We were flying out at 3:30, and received our sons passport at 1:00! Impossible to find an apoitment online? just come to a passport agency nearest to you without appointment, if you have valid reasons for this express service, and come very early, they will help you. We came to LA agency at 5 am, and there were already 6 people in line! (Agency in Tuscon, AZ doesn't have such long lines, from what I hear) But this was a line for people with appointment. So when it opened at 7am, we were moved to a different line. To get an appointment, get in line to the windows with WILL CALL sign.! So when our turn came, they asked us why we need the express passport, we showed tickets for the same day and got an appointment rights away ( this took less then 5 min), but needed to get through the other line which moved pretty quickly, and at 10:00 we were already out with receipt to get out passport at 1pm. We paid $175 for a child's passport, exactly the amount you find online, I don't know why the other reviewers paid 400$, maybe adult passports are that much more expensive. <name>Ik-Jung Kim< /name><rate>5<//rate><gmapID>0x80c2bb7d714a4885:0x37594b4563f90cf1< /gmapID>< review>
I am not a big reviewer, but I want to take a moment to compliment their service. The passport application for my daughter was still in progress after submission 4 weeks ago and the flight was next business day. It was impossible to get a hold of customer service by the phone (put me on hold more than 2 hours), and the online appointments were immediately full after every midnight. So I decided to drive 500 miles to the LA office to see if there is any solution.

It turned out that they do not accept walk-ins, so do not expect to be accepted without appointments. However, the manager came outside the building and helped people outside make appointments for next business day. In my case, they couldn't get access to my application because they found out mine was held up in the east coast. However, the manager kindly emailed the Charleston office and explained my urgency. A few hours later, the passport was mailed and arrived home next morning!

One more thing, I know it is really frustrating to see things don't work as you planned/wished but please be nice to them. They are good people and willing to help you with what they can. Some people are just so rude.<//review>

I think your experience at this agency all depends on when you come and how desperate you are.  If you come the same day as your flight, you are amazed that you can get a passport the same day.  If you come two weeks before your flight with an Appt., but you still have to stand for over an hour in the cold outside (In Feb, or heat in July), and then you have to come back and have over an hour wait at the pickup window (which may have had less than 10 people the day you came to wait in the application line, while that line suddenly has no wait), then you don‚Äôt see it as very efficient.  Regardless, come early, dress warmly (or have layers to lose), bring an umbrella and something to do.  There may be no line for your purpose that day...or you may spend over 3 hrs handling something you paid a premium for...just be prepared- no rhyme or reason. It ebbs and flows.<//Text>

< Text>
The PRO: You WILL get your passport the same day
The CON: It will take 9+ hours...everything is outside no lounge (sun, wind etc).

I showed up at 6 am (opens at 7 am) and there were 30 people in line. My flight was leaving the next day at 11 am. I was "low priority" and was processed to come back at  3pm once I handed in my filled out D form, pictures and the $170 fee at the window. The "high priority" were people leaving the same day. So you're likely to get your passport faster if your flight is the same day. The sooner the flight the highest priority and they are very good at parsing people out  from the line even before the office opens. Show up EARLY!< /Text>

<Review>My appt was at 1230PM on a Monday and I started out in security line at 12PM. Waited approx 10-15 min. After security I walked to the passport agency inside where I gave my confirmation # info. Then I waited in line to get my docs checked (maybe 10 minutes). Armando (first person I met within passport office) is responsible for checking you have all your needed documents before giving you a calling number to finalise & confirm new passport with federal official. I had some mistakes & he gave me time, paper, pen, and advice on how to fill things out efficiently, despite there being a line behind me he was extremely warm and his help really made my day, he went out of his way to make sure everything was perfect.
Make SURE YOU BRING ALL YOUR NEEDED DOCUMENTS - CORRECT PASSPORT PIC - FLIGHT RESERVATIONS - ETC.. reading these reviews it seems a lot of people did not look at what they actually needed to prepare.
The federal official read through everything & I signed a form and paid - I was in and out in about an hour.
Passport ready 3 days after appt for a flight a week from appt. So much more efficient & less annoying staff than you'd expect at a government office, fab experience overall.
Note: there may be loud kids / babies so I would advise bringing some headphones to pass the time waiting. Additionally for passport pickup there is no seating area, it's a window outside the building, so for those who have difficulty standing for possibly a long amount of time bring a foldup chair 8-)<//Review>< Pictures>

<time>1436200682533<//time><rating>4<//rating>< Review>
If you are traveling the same day get here early and by early I mean 5:30 AM!!! Because I got here at 6:45 am on a Tuesday and there were like 60 people ahead of me. You don't have to have an appointment but they do serve the appointments first.
Have your stuff ready like citizenship certificate, itinerary, passport forms filled out, passport picture, check, or credit card. You will not need all of these at once but just be ready.
1. Free parking
2. Sit and wait till they open at 7am
3. An officer will come and ask who has an appointment an then you'll be in a separate line
If you don't have an appointment remain at the same line. I didn't so I waited to be call to the window outside.
4. When you get to the window you'll let the person know what is your situation. I was applying for a brand new passport and was traveling within four days so they gave me a cheap piece of paper that said walk-in and the date
5. Then you'll go to another line and wait to be checked by security. This took long like 45 min since they let the appointments go first!
6. When the officers call you they give you a gray bin so you put everything there.
7. Now you're inside the building and you have to wait again to get a ticket with a number like the DMV. You tell the agent your situation and they issue your number. The good thing is that they have 18 windows. For the most part like 12-14 were servicing people. But I noticed that around 9ish a lot of agents took s break and so there were only 4 windows open. My number came up really fast. The agent asked if this was the first time I applying for a passport and asked for my itinerary and then I paid and he gave me a receipt. He told me to come pick up my passport on Thursday after 2pm or Monday around 8.

Additional info:
There's a place in the same vicinity that takes passport pics but only accept cash!! There's also food if you get hungry but is pricy. If you're unable to pick up your passport then you may authorize someone else to pick it up for you just follow the instruction on the receipt.
Overall I had a great experience!</Review>

<user_id>104516246447294995004</user_id><username>Gina Fetman< /username><Date>1537806578484< /Date>< rating>
4< /rating>
< text>
My usual nail salon is closed on Mondays and I needed a manicure for an event the next day, so I ended up at Polka Dot Nails after seeing a ton of great reviews online.
Service was friendly. The inside didn't have music blaring like some places and it was calming & quiet even though it was packed. The massage chair worked well and everything seemed clean and the color selection was good. I got a regular spa pedicure and a gel polish manicure.
The pedicure was good, no complaints. Basic and everything a spa pedicure usually entails.
The manicure cost less than my normal place that Only does gel which was fine, but now I know why- One of my nails (so, with GEL polish) Chipped after 2 days. (Gel polish is designed to Not do that.)
So, that's a bit frustrating. Plus, the UV gel dryers- both if then were having issues that day and I wonder if the polish didn't get to set correctly/thoroughly (?) there has to be a reason for the polish chipping because it's definitely not due to extensive wear & tear on my part. So that's my only real "complaint" - which is more so just a minor annoyance not a complaint. The experience as a whole and regarding the actual salon was not "bad" at all.
Cons: The parking lot is really tiny, and they ONLY take cash tips so I had to go across the street to find an ATM so I could tip. Granted, they took me as a walk -in and I didn't have to wait even though they were quite busy.
Pros: It's a good nail salon and I would go there again if the need arose, friendly & thorough service (no rushing to get me in & out or not doing a good job due to rushing)
...but even as I type this I'm looking at my chipped nail and feeling a little bit salty about it. I didn't spend $30 on a manicure to have it last 48 hours....<//text>

Ive eaten here twice, on my second visit I remembered right away why I hadnt returned sooner ( over a year). While on social media I got an add for thier pulled pork and decided I wanted to try it. I went on Tuesday and of course the pulled pork was only a special on a certain day. I wear contact's and have pretty good eyesight but that doesn't help read the menu. Its literally the smallest writing ive ever seen for a menu making paneras menu look like large font. I couod look past all that if the food was on point. But unfortunately it's not, I dont understand why an order of fried zucchini comes in a family size, and with no ranch to dip it in. I ordered 2 additional ranches assuming id have 4 of the small containers. The two I recieved didnt last long at all. More importantly I and my partner probably ate 1/3 the rest was wasted. I ordered a pastrami sandwich which was the only tasty part of my $25 meal the french roll was very soft and the meat was cooked perfectly. Thats the only reason im giving them 2 stars. Considering how large the zucchini portion was the french frys pprtion that came with my sandwich combo was measly and they were terrible not salted. I wasnt offered any salt or pepper, not even ketchup. Luckily I had some spare packets in my car. Lastly but most disgusting was the fountain drink. I will never be eating here again or at least anytime soon</review>
